mysql> select 
    -> g.species as Species,
    -> g.accession as Accession,
    -> g.genename as Gene, 
    -> m.start as Position,
    -> round(m.mfe,2) as MFE,
    -> m.pairs as Pairs,
    -> round(b.mfe_mean,2) as MeanMFE,
    -> round(b.mfe_sd,2) as StdevMFE,
    -> round((m.mfe - b.mfe_mean)/b.mfe_sd,2) as zR,
    -> round(b.pairs_mean,2) as MeanPairs,
    -> round(b.pairs_sd,2) as StdevPairs,
    -> round((m.pairs - b.pairs_mean)/b.pairs_sd,2) as zP,
    -> m.slipsite as SlipperySite,
    -> m.sequence as StructureSequence,
    -> m.parsed as BasePairs,
    -> m.algorithm as FoldingAlgorithm
    -> from 
    -> genome as g,
    -> mfe as m,
    -> boot as b
    -> where
    -> m.algorithm = "pknots" and
    -> m.mfe = ( select min(mfe) from mfe where accession = m.accession and start = m.start ) and
    -> m.mfe <= -17.30 and
    -> (m.mfe - b.mfe_mean)/b.mfe_sd <= -1.65 and 
    -> g.species = "saccharomyces_cerevisiae" and
    -> g.id = m.genome_id and
    -> m.id = b.mfe_id 
    -> group by accession,start
    -> ;
